				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Gott fähret auf mit Jauchzen, BWV 43 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 11 movements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Gott fähret auf mit Jauchzen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">God is gone up with Jubilation
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/181021469">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gott_f%C3%A4hret_auf_mit_Jauchzen,_BWV_43">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/181021469">181021469</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300007264">300007264</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13909597w">13909597w</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 43&#160;; BC A 77
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 251
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>C major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 11 movements):
<dl><dt><ul><li>Erster Teil
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Chorus: Gott fähret auf mit Jauchzen (C major)
</dd><dd>2. Recitativo (Tenor): Es will der Höchste sich ein Siegsgepräng (A minor-G major)
</dd><dd>3. Aria (Tenor): Ja tausendmal tausend begleiten den Wagen (G major)
</dd><dd>4. Recitativo (Soprano): Und der Herr, nachdem er mit ihnen geredet hatte (E minor)
</dd><dd>5. Aria (Soprano): Mein Jesus hat nunmehr (E minor)
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Zweiter Teil
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>6. Recitativo (Bass): Es kommt der Helden Held (C major)
</dd><dd>7. Aria (Bass): Er ists, der ganz allein (C major)
</dd><dd>8. Recitativo (Alto): Der Vater hat ihm ja (A minor)
</dd><dd>9. Aria (Alto): Ich sehe schon im Geist (A minor)
</dd><dd>10. Recitativo (Soprano): Er will mir neben sich (G major-E minor)
</dd><dd>11. Chorale: Du Lebensfürst, Herr Jesu Christ (G major)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1726 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1726-05-30 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1863 (BGA) or before
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd>Psalm XLVII: 6-7 (No.1)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Anonymous" title="Category:Anonymous">Anonymous</a> (Nos.2-3, 5-10)<br />Mark 16: 19 (No.4)<br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Rist,_Johann" title="Category:Rist, Johann">Johann Rist</a> (1607-1667) (No.11)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>

</li><li> BWV 222: <i>Mein Odem ist schwach</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Ernst" title="Category:Bach, Johann Ernst">Johann Ernst Bach</a>)
</li><li> BWV 223: <i>Meine Seele soll Gott loben</i>
</li><li> BWV 224: <i>Reisst euch los, bekränkte Sinnen</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Carl_Philipp_Emanuel" title="Category:Bach, Carl Philipp Emanuel">Carl Philipp Emanuel Bach</a>?)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
</td></tr></table>
